 wdgStop();
 wdgStart(type);
 reStartPusher();
 e.preventDefault();
 sendGAEvent("hp_market_widget", "change_tab-" + type);
 return false;
 });

 // var type = $('.js-nav_type_for_chart:first').data('type');

 wdgStart('Most');
 reStartPusher();

 wdgStop();
 reStartPusher();

 $('[data-frame]', iwrap).on('click', function(){

 if(f){
 $('.active[data-frame]', iwrap).removeClass('active');
 $(this).addClass('active');
 chart.setTimeframe(f);
 sendGAEvent("hp_market_widget", "change_frame");
 }

 $('[data-iid],[data-iid-tmp]', iwrap).on('click', function(){
 var iid = $(this).data('iid');
 iid = iid ? iid : $(this).data('iid-tmp');
 if(iid){
 $('.active[data-iid],.active[data-iid-tmp]', iwrap).removeClass('active');
 $(this).addClass('active');
 chart.setMarket(iid, $(this).data('dg'));
 sendGAEvent("hp_market_widget", "change_market");
 reStartPusher();
 }
 });
 function wdgStart(type){
 $('.js-type-' + type, iwrap).children('[data-iid-tmp]').each(function(){
 $(this).attr('data-iid', $(this).data('iid-tmp'));
 });
 $('.js-type-' + type, iwrap).removeClass('hidden').addClass('active').children().first().click();
 $('.view-btn-wrap > .button-link.js-type-' + type, iwrap).removeClass('hidden');
 };
 function wdgStop(){
 $('.view-btn-wrap > .button-link', iwrap).addClass('hidden');
 $('.js-tools__list', iwrap).addClass('hidden').removeClass('active');
 $('[data-iid]', iwrap).removeAttr('data-iid');
 };
 function reStartPusher(){
 livePricesunSubscribe();
 livePricesSubscribe();
 };
 };

 function agregateMonth(arr){

 var year;

 high = v.high;

 if(low > v.low){

 open = v.open;
 }
 });
 return agregatedArr;

 var delimiter = ',';

 delimiter = "&nbsp";
 }else if(['de','da','el','hr','id','it','ro','sl'].includes(ln)){
 delimiter = ".";

 function animateValue(obj, start, end, duration) {
 var startTimestamp = null;
 var dd;
 const step = (timestamp) => {
 if (!startTimestamp) startTimestamp = timestamp;
 const progress = Math.min((timestamp - startTimestamp) / duration, 1);
 dd = Math.floor(progress * (end - start) + start);
 obj.innerHTML = dd.toString().replace(/\B(?=(\d{3})+(?!\d))/g, delimiter);
 if (progress < 1) {
 window.requestAnimationFrame(step);
 }
 };
 window.requestAnimationFrame(step);
 }
 var allObj = $(".cc-counter span[data-count]");
 const callbacksCounterBanner = () => {
 allObj.each(function(index) {
 animateValue(this, 0, $(this).data('count'), 5000);
 });
 }
 var targetCounterBanner = document.querySelectorAll('.js-counter')
 observeEl(targetCounterBanner, callbacksCounterBanner, {threshold: 0.5});
 };

 window.pageReadyFN.push(initFn_counter);

 function modalCalculator(){
 var depth = 365;
 var action = 'buy';
 var instruments = {"13863591790794066":{"price_buy":"87.60","price_sell":"84.60","digits":"2","startPrice":"84.63","price_date":"2023-03-26","quotedCurrency":"EUR","marginStr":"1:50","margin":2,"margins":[1,2]}};
 var instrument = instruments["13863591790794066"];
 var investmentsMap = [20,100,500,1000,10000];
 var slider = $('.js-tradingCalcRange', wrap);
 var marginStr = $('.js-marginStrOut', wrap);
 var invest = $('.js-investOut', wrap);
 var result = $('.js-resultOut', wrap);
 var dateFromOut = $('.js-dateFromOut', wrap);
 var dateToOut = $('.js-dateToOut', wrap);
 var priceFromOut = $('.js-priceFromOut', wrap);
 var priceToOut = $('.js-priceToOut', wrap);
 var currencyOut = $('.js-currencyOut', wrap);
 var marginsOut = $('.js-marginsOut', wrap);
 var tradeSize = $('.js-tradeSizeOut', wrap);
 var instrumentSelect = $('.js-marketSelected', wrap);
 var marginSelect = $('.js-marginSelect', wrap);
 var investSelect = $('.js-investSelect', wrap);
 var actionSelect = $('.js-action', wrap);
 var instrumentPlaceholderOut = $('.js-instrumentName', wrap);
 var currency = '$';
 setCurrency();
 var currentHistory;
 var dataFrom;
 var dataTo;
 var needFindBestInstr = true;
 var profitInstruments = new Map();
 var validInstr = [];
 var initRange = function(){
 var stepFrom,
 stepTo;
 currentHistory = chart.chartData;
 if(dataFrom && dataFrom.t && dataTo && dataTo.t){
 stepFrom = currentHistory.findIndex(x => x.t === dataFrom.t);
 stepTo = currentHistory.findIndex(x => x.t === dataTo.t);
 if(stepFrom == -1 || stepTo == -1){
 stepFrom = Math.round((currentHistory.length - 1) * 0.2);
 stepTo = Math.round((currentHistory.length - 1) * 0.8);
 }
 }else{
 stepFrom = Math.round((currentHistory.length - 1) * 0.2);
 stepTo = Math.round((currentHistory.length - 1) * 0.8);
 }
 if(!stepTo || !stepFrom){
 wrap.addClass('hidden');
 return;
 }
 slider.slider('option',{max: currentHistory.length - 1,values: [stepFrom, stepTo]});
 updateSlider();
 if(needFindBestInstr){
 selectBestInstrument();
 }
 }
 slider.slider({
 range: true,
 min: 0,
 slide: function() {
 updateSlider();
 sendGAEvent("calculator", "click_daterange");
 }
 });
 var chart = createChart($('.js-tradingCalcChart', wrap).find('canvas').get(0), {livePrices: false, theme: 'simpleGray', exitFn: initRange, depth: depth});
 chart.setMarket('13863591790794066', 2);
 function setCurrency(){
 if(instrument['quotedCurrency'] == 'EUR'){
 currency = '€';
 }else{
 currency = '$';
 }
 }
 function updateSlider(){
 if(currentHistory){
 var sliderPositionFrom = slider.slider( "values", 0 );
 var sliderPositionTo = slider.slider( "values", 1 );
 dataFrom = currentHistory[sliderPositionFrom];
 dataTo = currentHistory[sliderPositionTo];
 var options = {
 year: 'numeric',
 month: 'numeric',
 day: 'numeric',
 timezone: 'UTC'
 };
 dateFromOut.text(TimeAgo.inWords(dataFrom.t, 'calculator'));
 dateToOut.text(TimeAgo.inWords(dataTo.t, 'calculator'));
 priceFromOut.text(dataFrom.y);
 priceToOut.text(dataTo.y);
 calculate();
 }
 }
 function updateVisibleFields(){
 var investValue = investmentsMap[investSelect.val() - 1];
 var marginValue = instrument.margins[marginSelect.val() - 1];
 var tradeSizeValue = investValue * marginValue;
 invest.text(investValue);
 marginStr.text(marginValue);
 tradeSize.text(tradeSizeValue);
 currencyOut.html(currency);
 calculate();
 }
 function calculate(){
 if(currentHistory){
 var res;
 if(action=='sell') {
 res = ( invest.text() * marginStr.text() / priceFromOut.text() * (priceFromOut.text() - priceToOut.text()) );
 }else{
 res = ( invest.text() * marginStr.text() / priceFromOut.text() * (priceToOut.text() - priceFromOut.text()) );
 }
 result.html(currency + res.toFixed(2));
 }
 }
 function getProfitByTime(proxyID, timestamp, target){
 if(!proxyID || !timestamp){
 return;
 }
 var q = {
 depth: 1,
 instrumentId: proxyID,
 timeframe: 'D1',
 timestamp: timestamp,
 };
 APICall("../../trading/v1/quoteHistory", q).then((d) => {
 if (d && d.history && d.history[0]) {
 profitInstruments.set(proxyID + '_' + target, d.history[0].close);
 if(validInstr.length * 2 == profitInstruments.size){
 changeToProfit();
 }
 }
 });
 }
 function selectBestInstrument(){
 needFindBestInstr = false;
 instrumentPlaceholderOut.removeAttr("data-url");
 var timeFrom = dataFrom.t / 1000;
 var timeTo = dataTo.t / 1000;
 instrumentSelect.each(function(i, v){
 var currentInstr = $(v).data('sort');
 var currentInstrUrl = $(v).data('url');
 if (currentInstr){
 validInstr.push({currentInstr, currentInstrUrl});
 getProfitByTime(currentInstr, timeFrom, 'open');
 getProfitByTime(currentInstr, timeTo, 'close');
 }
 });
 }
 function changeToProfit(){
 var maxProfit = -100500;
 var bestIid;
 var bestUrl;
 $.each(validInstr, function(i, v){
 var open = profitInstruments.get(v.currentInstr + '_open');
 var close = profitInstruments.get(v.currentInstr + '_close');
 var maxMargin = instruments[v.currentInstr].margins[instruments[v.currentInstr].margins.length - 1];
 var prof = ( invest.text() * maxMargin / open * (close - open) );
 if (maxProfit < prof){
 maxProfit = prof;
 bestIid = v.currentInstr;
 bestUrl = v.currentInstrUrl;
 }
 });
 var instrName = $('[data-sort=' + bestIid + ']', wrap).text();
 instrumentPlaceholderOut.attr('placeholder', instrName);
 if (devicePr != 'iphone' && devicePr != 'android' && devicePr != 'uu') {
 document.querySelector(".js-btn_calculator").setAttribute("href", "https://capitalcom.onelink.me/700515151?af_dp=https%3A%2F%2Fcapital.com%2Finstrument%3Fid%3D" + bestIid + "&&cp_device_id=oyq1s6ps-ttos-941q-hrx1-7l8t2g2li5eh");
 }else if(devicePr == 'uu') {
 document.querySelector(".js-btn_calculator").setAttribute("href", "/trading/platform/spotlight/" + bestIid + "?side=sell");
 }
 if(bestIid){
 changeInstr(bestIid);
 }
 }
 function changeInstr(proxyID){
 instrument = instruments[proxyID];
 setCurrency();
 var mrgns = instrument.margins;
 marginSelect.attr('max', mrgns.length);
 marginSelect.attr('value', mrgns[mrgns.length - 1]);
 marginSelect.attr('style', '--max: ' + mrgns.length);
 marginsOut.html('<li>' + mrgns.join( ":1</li><li>" ) + ':1</li>' );
 updateVisibleFields();
 chart.setMarket(proxyID);
 }
 actionSelect.on('click', function(){

xlink:href="/images/spriteSvg/common.svg?v=20230323_115722#arrowLong"></use> </svg> </div> <p><span>Les CFD sont des instruments complexes et présentent des risques élevés de perte rapide de capital en raison de l&#39;effet de levier.</span><span class=text-accord> <span class=txt-bold><strong>84% des comptes des investisseurs particuliers perdent de l&#39;argent quand ils tradent sur les CFD avec ce fournisseur</strong>.</span> Il faut s&#39;assurer que vous comprenez le principe de ces CFD et que vous pouvez vous permettre de prendre des risques en perdant votre argent.</span> <a href=/risk-disclosure-policy target=_blank>Déclaration de divulgation des risques</a></p> <p>La valeur des actions et des ETF achetés via un compte de trading d&#39;actions peut aussi bien baisser qu&#39;augmenter. Cela signifie que vous pouvez récupérer moins que ce que vous avez initialement investi. Les performances passées ne garantissent pas les résultats futurs.</p> <p>Avertissement concernant les risques : les transactions sans instruments de gré à gré non livrables constituent une activité risquée et peuvent certes générer des gains, mais également des pertes. Le montant de la perte potentielle est limité aux fonds que nous détenons pour vous et en votre nom, en relation avec votre compte de trading. Les gains passés ne garantissent pas des gains à venir. Utilisez les services de formation de notre entreprise pour comprendre les risques avant de commencer toute opération.</p> <p>Capital Com SV Investments Limited est une société chypriote enregistrée sous le numéro HE 354252. Cependant, avec le trading traditionnel, vous concluez un contrat pour \u00e9changer la propri\u00e9t\u00e9 l\u00e9gale des actions individuelles ou des marchandises contre de l'argent, et vous en poss\u00e9dez jusqu'\u00e0 ce que vous le vendiez \u00e0 nouveau. br \/]\nCFD sont des produits \u00e0 effet de levier, ce qui signifie que vous n'avez qu'\u00e0 d\u00e9poser un pourcentage de la valeur totale du trading CFD pour ouvrir une position.
